Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Cathode Ray Adjustment Indicator 250

— Yi Zhi

Currently, superheterodyne receivers with advanced selectivity are increasingly developed. A tuning indicator is much needed to visually inspect and adjust the radio signal to the sharpest sensitivity point. After British exploration and research, a kind of cathode ray adjustment tube was obtained, named the "Adjustment Imaging Tube" (Junograph). The shape of this tube is shown in Figure 1, like an ordinary vacuum tube. There are filaments, screen grids, and a fluorite light screen (Fluorescent Screen and a pair of bias plates) inside the tube.

When using it, the filament is connected to a four-volt voltage. After the radio is working...

Fig. 1 Fluorite Bias Plate ( ) Plate Terminal British Five-Tube 251

...a fluorite light spot and a short fluorite light line are emitted on the fluorite light screen inside the glass tube to adjust the signal to the best point.

This device is actually the smallest cathode ray oscillograph. It is connected to the last stage of the intermediate frequency (Intermediate Frequen5y) of a superheterodyne receiver... There are two connection methods [>I

R4 Connect Detector 5000 Fig. 2 252

See Figures 2(A) and (B). In Figure (A), a bleeder resistor R is required, with a resistance of 10,000 or 20,000 ohms. This bleeder resistor R is connected in series with the last intermediate frequency tube. Therefore, a small green light spot, similar to fluorescence, is seen on the fluorite light screen. This light spot is biased to the left before the signal is adjusted. After the signal is adjusted, it moves to the right. The stronger the signal, the more it is biased to the right.

Figure 2(B) shows another connection method for using the tube. This adjustment imaging tube is connected to the last adjustment stage of the radio, and a line of short, interconnected green lines is emitted on the fluorite light screen. The longer the line, the stronger the signal.

This simple cathode ray oscillograph has other uses besides being used as a tuning indicator, which will not be described in detail here.

New Type of Compound Vacuum Tube 253

— Ban Jie

Since the beginning, vacuum tubes are divided into categories such as rectifier tubes, detector tubes, and amplifier tubes because of the different functions. Because the old-fashioned vacuum tube can only have one function, and at the same time, it can only serve two or more functions. If there are any, they must be further modified in the circuit (such as in the case of regenerative circuits) before the purpose of the multiple functions can be achieved, but this is not common. In recent years, with the advancement of the vacuum tube industry, compound vacuum tubes have emerged to meet the needs of the times. Therefore, we only need to prepare one new type of vacuum tube to be able to serve two or more functions at the same time.

Figure 1 A Triode Section Compound Diode Section 2RGTOPCF16PH543 254

(Tube Pole Triode Double)

B Pentode Section Compound Diode Section 7P2SC1P26P1543HGTOP 255

Tube Pole Pentode Double

The so-called compound vacuum tubes are compound diodes and triodes such as UZ55, U2Z75, UZ85, 2A6, etc., and compound diodes and pentodes such as 2B7, 6B7, etc. Its symbol is shown in Figure 1. A compound diode and triode (as shown in Figure A) has a compound diode section and a triode section in a glass tube. A compound diode and pentode has a compound diode section and a pentode section in a glass tube. The so-called compound diode section is composed of a common cathode and two screen grids (P2, P3). The so-called triode section is equivalent to an ordinary triode, and the so-called pentode is equivalent to an ordinary pentode. The two parts in the glass tube all share a cathode. The structure of each electrode is shown in Figure 2. The lower part is the compound diode section, and the upper part is the triode section (or pentode section). There is a shielding element S in the middle to shield the electrons of the two parts. This point is very different from other vacuum tubes.

Figure 2 Triode Section Shielding Element Compound Diode Section GPSCP1P2H256361 256

Tube Pole Triode Double Configuration Diagram Use a tube socket. For compound diodes and triodes, a U2 type six-pin socket is used, while compound diodes and pentodes use

UT type (small) seven-pin socket. The configuration of each electrode is as shown in Figures 3 A and B.

Figure 3 B (1) (2) (3) (4) (5) (6) (7) 257

A (1) (2) (3) (4) (5) (6) 258

Depending on the different connection methods, the compound diode section can be used for half-wave detection, full-wave detection, automatic volume control (A·V·C·) or both. The detection current after detection in the compound diode section is directly introduced into the triode section (or pentode section) to perform audio frequency amplification. In ordinary detector tubes, the external signal is amplified at the same time it is detected; however, in this type of new tube, the detection and amplification functions are performed separately in the compound diode section and the triode section (or pentode section). This is a characteristic that distinguishes the new tube from the old tube.

The circuit in Figure 4 connects the two screen grids of the compound diode section in parallel to perform half-wave detection. The detection current is then directly introduced into the triode section to perform

Audio frequency amplification, and it also serves as automatic volume control. If there is a signal input, the two ends of the two resistors R1 and R2 will follow the size of the detection current and

Figure 4 LF R1 R2 (A, V, C) Negative Voltage of the Previous Vacuum Tube Negative Voltage of the Triode Section Negative Voltage of the Previous Vacuum Tube 259

Produce a high or low voltage drop to achieve the function of automatic volume control.

Using this tube, a one-tube radio can be made, and its effectiveness is better than that of an old-fashioned two-tube radio. Due to space limitations, I will describe it in detail for readers in the next issue.

Shortwave Knowledge 260

Wei Xin Su...

Today's radio broadcasting is most respected for shortwave because shortwave can reach extremely far distances with less power, and the static electricity that is most annoying and most difficult to avoid in radio communications is also less interfering. Conversely, on the receiving side, if you want to listen to broadcasts from Europe and the United States, it is impossible without shortwave.

There are now many shortwave radios in the country, but the changes and mysteries of shortwave communication cannot be compared with longwave (broadcast waveband). If you have no common sense about receiving radio on shortwave, you will inevitably be disappointed.

The so-called shortwave refers to wavelengths shorter than the ordinary broadcast waveband, that is, wavelengths below 200 meters to about 15 meters.

Shortwave radios usually have three or four or more coils for receiving wavebands of different lengths. However, these various wavelengths are affected by various reasons, so some are conducive to receiving during the day, and some cannot be received until night.

Difference between Day and Night

Receiving telecommunications at wavelengths below 25 meters is usually better during the day than at night. But the opposite is true for wavelengths above 50 meters. According to experiments, for wavelengths below 20 meters, the entire path from the broadcasting station to the receiving machine must be in daylight to be able to listen. Between 20 meters and 35 meters, it is best to have the broadcasting machine or the radio in the dark.

Skywave and Groundwave

Radio receivers have skywave and groundwave. Receiving sound via groundwave is very reliable, but the distance that can be received is shorter. Receiving via skywave can receive very long distances, but it is affected by seasonal climate and the change between day and night, and it can also produce large skip distances, making it impossible for people in this area to listen.

The meaning of skip distance refers to an area that groundwave cannot reach and skywave has not reached. Receiving in this area will not achieve good results, or even nothing will be heard. The skip distance is not fixed and changes from day to night. This is also a major reason why shortwave reception is sometimes good and sometimes bad.

Receiving by groundwave, if there is no steel-framed building isolation and local interference is too severe, the results should always be good. The reliable distance for groundwave reception is approximately 90 miles for a wavelength of 100 meters and only 15 miles for a wavelength of 15 meters. Shortwave telecommunications are usually received by skywave, and very few are received by groundwave. The reliable path of skywave reception must be transferred according to the season and day and night. For wavelengths of 100 meters, it is approximately between 90 miles and 2,500 miles; for 25 meters, it starts from 300 miles to infinity; for 15 meters, it is approximately 700 to 4,000 miles at noon. At midnight, wavelengths below 15 meters can only be received within the range reached by groundwave. For wavelengths below 7.5 meters, there is no so-called skywave, and its broadcasting principle is close to the emission of light waves.

The changes in the reliable range of skywave are very slow between seasons, but very rapid between day and night. The skip distance is the smallest during the day and the largest at midnight. Listeners are most likely to encounter rare situations during the time when sunrise and sunset change the most. The shorter the wavelength, the larger the skip distance. In addition, reasons such as static electricity, sunspots, and magnetic storms can all affect the receiving distance. (To be continued)

Design and Principles of Car Radios 261

— KMK

The speaker C838RH3GL3L239L1XXC2C5R3R6R2C3R5CAR6C7AFCC9D10CKMK connects to a six-volt storage battery. The lights are all connected to X. 262

Car radios are not yet popular in our country. Although there are car radios for sale in Shanghai, the price is so expensive that ordinary people cannot afford them. Even the installation in cars is very rare. Its special feature is that the power supply is provided by a six-volt storage battery, and the B voltage is also increased by the power of the six-volt storage battery. The power supply of the storage battery is DC, and the DC voltage can only be reduced but cannot be increased. If you want to increase it, you must first convert DC to AC. (As shown in the attached diagram) Therefore, a DC-to-AC vibrating machine is added to the machine to turn the stable DC power supply into a kind of pulsating AC, and then connected to the primary stage of the step-up transformer, and then it undergoes a process of rectification and filtering to become a stable high-voltage current again (that is, B voltage). As for the vibrating machine in the machine, it can also be designed according to this issue 42 (How to use a transformer for DC), the other parts are largely the same. The antenna can use a piece of 48-inch by 36-inch red copper wire cloth sandwiched in the car's canopy. The ground wire can be connected to the negative electrode of the storage battery. The machine uses 39 for business cycle amplification, 36 for detection, 38 for powerful low amplification, and 8 for full-wave rectification. The manufacturing method of the step-up transformer (T) is slightly different from that of ordinary transformers. The wire used for winding the coil must use double-yarn wrapping (do not use enameled wire). Each layer must be separated by thicker insulation, and do not loosen it. Because magnetic feeling will occur in the coil when the vibrating machine vibrates, if the inner coil vibrates slightly, it will shorten its life. The primary stage of the transformer is 5 volts, and the secondary high voltage is 160 volts at both ends. After rectification and filtering, there are more than 130 volts left for amplification. The filament poles of the vacuum tube are directly connected to the storage battery. L uses No. 30 enameled wire to wind 30 turns on a half-inch diameter rubber tube. A distance of one-quarter inch from L winds 90 turns for L1. L2 is the same as L, L3 is the same as L1. C1 and C2 are .00035MF fixed capacitors, C4 is .5MF fixed capacitor, C5 is .0001MF fixed capacitor, C6 is .02MF fixed capacitor, C7 is .4MF fixed capacitor, C8, C9, C10, and C11 are all 4MF fixed capacitors, R1 is a 150-ohm fixed bleeder resistor, R2 is a 200,000-ohm variable bleeder resistor with a switch (S) to turn on the filament and the power of the vibrating machine, R3 is a 50,000-ohm fixed bleeder resistor, R4 is a 55,000-ohm fixed bleeder resistor, R6 is a 1,600-ohm fixed bleeder resistor, and AFC self-inductance is 30 Henry, which can pass a current of 30 amperes. The dotted line in the attached diagram is the overall isolation shield to eliminate noise.

The Reason Why Radio Waves Are Weaker During the Day and Stronger at Night 263

— Bo Qing

Let's talk about why the radio reception strength is stronger at night than during the day for long-distance radio reception. The reason is very simple.

Because the radio waves emitted by the transmitting antenna can be roughly divided into two types: one is propagated along the Earth's surface, called the surface wave; the other is propagated to the sky, called the sky wave.

Since the surface wave is propagated from the Earth's surface, it will naturally cause a rapid attenuation phenomenon, so it is very difficult to propagate it to a long distance.

As for the sky wave, since it is propagated through space, it is bound to be affected by the state of space.

The air above the Earth gradually thins out as the altitude increases. Therefore, the natural gases that exist in the upper layer are various thin gases. These gases are ionized by the action of sunlight and are imagined to form a layer, which is called the Heaviside Layer.

During the day, because there is strong sunlight, this layer is relatively close to the Earth's surface, and the sky wave will naturally lose most of its power when it encounters it. However, at night, because the ionosphere moves far upward, the sky wave must undergo reflection and refraction when it wants to reach the upper part from here, and most of it will inevitably reach a place farther away from the Earth's surface again.

When receiving radio, only surface waves are received during the day, so long-distance radio reception is naturally very weak. However, once it is night, as mentioned above, the sky wave comes from the sky, so the radio reception strength will naturally increase.

A Self-Made Economical Variable Capacitor 264

— Zhang Zongrong

A variable capacitor is quite important in radio. The ones sold on the market are very expensive. One machine often needs one to several of them. The general comrades who like to study radio but are limited by economics have a sigh of regret. Now there is a variable capacitor that can be made for only a few cents, so I will share it with the aforementioned comrades.

Figure 1 Hard Cardboard Tin Wire Figure 2 Wax Paper Figure 3 ( 265

<I. ]

Cut 11 pieces of cardboard into the shape shown in Figure 1 (the number of pieces can be determined according to individual needs). Cut 11 pieces of tinplate from the cigarette box into rectangles, glue them to the right end of the cardboard, and punch a small hole at the × position. Insert a 3-inch-long bare copper wire (i.e., yarn-colored wire with the outer coating removed) and fold both ends to wrap them tightly. Glue each piece of foreign wax paper (Figure 2) together. After all 11 pieces have been made, twist all the wire ends into one wire end and solder it with tin. This is the fixed piece.

Figure 4 Figure 5 Figure 6 266

There are ten moving pieces, and the size of each piece is half of the fixed piece (Figure 3). Make them as before.

Outer shell (Figure 4), same size as the fixed piece. Outer shell (Figure 5), the protruding part around is the edge, and the dashed line is rubbed into a deep pattern. Punch a small hole at the × position to expose the wire end of the fixed piece.

After each item is made, stack the fixed and moving pieces alternately, and put them into the shell (Figure 6). When using, connect the two wire ends to the inside of the machine, and moving the moving pieces outward will obtain the required wavelength. (End)

Shortwave Radio and Capacitors 267

— Yong Yan

Although capacitors in radios can sometimes be omitted, the effect of installing them is better. Fixed capacitors are especially important in shortwave machines. Now I will describe the places where fixed capacitors should be installed in shortwave radios, the capacitance of the capacitors, and the effects after installation:

(1) Connect a .0005 megafarad fixed capacitor across the secondary stage of the first audio frequency transformer to make the tone mellow.

(2) Connect a .002 to .001 megafarad capacitor across the primary stage of the first audio frequency transformer to enhance the regeneration force of the regenerative shortwave radio.

(3) Connecting a 1 megafarad fixed capacitor between the positive and negative poles of the B battery can increase the receiving range and volume. (If the B voltages used in the detection stage and the audio frequency amplification stage are different, it is advisable to connect a 1 megafarad fixed capacitor to each.)

(4) Connecting a .0005 to .001 megafarad fixed capacitor at the output of the radio can reduce noise.

(5) If a variable resistor is used to adjust the regenerative force, if a .005 megafarad fixed capacitor is connected between the radio frequency choke (R, F, C,) connected to one end of the regeneration coil and the negative pole of the B battery, noise can be reduced and sensitivity can be increased.

Records of Drifting Fragrance from the Imperial Incense 270

— Original work by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

Imagine, dear reader: a stoker with a soot-blackened face, constantly surrounded by smoke and coal, wearing a small, parasol-like court hat. Doesn't he look exactly like a wizened old mushroom? Now, compare his pair of black satin boots, his robe of colors as vibrant as a rainbow, and the coal pile he stands beside, and you can easily imagine what a sight that would be! But this scene actually happened. After all, the Empress Dowager's orders were law, and who could change them!

Inside a locomotive, there were three drivers on duty at the same time. Of course, they were all dressed like eunuchs. Let us distinguish them as Driver A, Driver B, and Driver C. At that time, their positions were as important as those of ministers in the court or governors of provinces. Therefore, they could freely request more assistants. However, in reality, only Driver A was actually driving the train. (In fact, two people were not allowed to drive at the same time.) On ordinary days, he would have a seat to sit on comfortably. However, on this imperial train, no one except the Empress Dowager herself was allowed to sit. Therefore, he had to stand upright. Driver B's job was very easy. He only needed to look ahead and watch for any changes on the tracks. For example, if a cow crossed the tracks, or other similar things, he was responsible for reporting to Driver A. This person did not exist on ordinary trains; or if he did, he could casually pull up a stool and sit next to Driver A. But this time, of course, he could no longer sit. Therefore, he often alternated between squatting and kneeling to rest a little. This was the etiquette and authority that the Empress Dowager paid the most attention to. (16)

Shanghai 271

— Wei Jing

In China, except for the production of antiquities, because Shanghai has no ancient tombs, Shanghai is more developed than any other place in almost everything else.

Speaking positively, the eighteen-story, twenty-four-story buildings are much taller than the ancient pagodas in famous mountains and ancient temples. Speaking of roads, you can drive in a car with all four wheels rolling on the road for ten or eight miles, and not a drop of water will spill from a cup inside the car. This is different from cars elsewhere, where people's buttocks are detached from the seats, like getting out of bed. Even the flat ones are mostly like the so-called "one-bump" roads in some places, which are just a small taste of the real thing. In terms of clothing, silk brocades and woolen fabrics are more plentiful and better than elsewhere. Even taking factory cloth as an example, the amount imported into the interior from Shanghai each year is countless. Eating is even more a collection of the best of the East and West, China and abroad, Beijing, Cantonese, Suzhou, and Yangzhou cuisines. It can be said that all kinds of dishes are available, and no taste is lacking. Finally, let's talk about culture. There are public, private, and even "wild chicken" universities. There are even more middle schools of all kinds. There are simply too many primary schools to list. On average, there is at least one primary school in every alley, although some are located in the kitchen.

Speaking negatively, opium dens, gambling dens, brothels, robbers, swindlers, kidnappers, everything is more developed than anywhere else. In addition, all kinds of bizarre things, such as suicides, offenses against public morals, and methods of promoting foreign goods, are also beyond the reach of other places.

It is said that the reason why Shanghai is Shanghai is because of these great places.

Wandering on the Bustling Streets 272

— Fu Yizhi

After Wednesday, I look forward to the arrival of Sunday. But when Sunday arrives, it is more boring than expected. It feels like working like a machine is more meaningful. This must be because the spirit has lost its support! However, the melting and eroding spring light, as lovely as a beautiful woman, is beckoning outside. Do you think I wouldn't be fascinated? "A moment of spring night is worth a thousand gold," I want to hold on to it. After all, I'm not old yet!

Ah! Where to go? I was stunned. I wandered, I wandered on this bustling, headache-inducing street. Where are the green grass, red flowers, and lush willows? Tall buildings flank a long, sleek road. The sun, like a maiden bound by so-called propriety, only reveals half of her beautiful face through the half-rolled beaded curtain. Trains, one carriage after another, are packed with countless machines for selling bread, rumbling and clanging as they move forward, move forward. Cars whiz by with a whoosh. Without dust, rickshaw pullers, sweating profusely, one, two, dragging young masters and misses with stretched legs, desperately rushing to their destinations. Arrogant "gentlemen," holding the tender lotus-like jade arms of playful girls, rush forward with a solemn air... Why? They, or they, wriggle, wriggle. I was stunned!

Spring has long arrived in the world. The azure sky, the warm sun, the fragrant flowers, the singing of birds in the branches. This beautiful nature, ah, I have no way to be close to it. I wander alone on the street where the sounds of cars and people intertwine. Here, too, is a symbol of the vitality of spring!

Looking to the Future (The God of Peace Begs the God of War for Mercy) 273

The Harmful Queue 274

— Zui Chi Sheng

The queue, among modern city ladies, can be considered to have been squeezed out and fallen behind by the word "modern." In fact, the queue, from a formal point of view, hangs down like a pig's tail, and has nothing beautiful about it. From a practical point of view, it snags and tangles, making it inconvenient to do things. It is really better to cut it off crisply and neatly. In particular, women from poor families who work must remove this harmful thing. Know that this queue is your enemy. Sometimes, it can even put you to death. But they have shallow knowledge and mostly hold old ideas, keeping this troublesome silk and refusing to cut it off. It is really pitiful and deplorable!

Not long ago, in the local news column of this newspaper, there was a record like this: "A female worker from Yangzhou, surnamed ×××, fifteen years old, at the ××× Japanese-Chinese Second Yarn Factory in this port, was working last night. By chance, her queue was suddenly caught in the machine belt, and she was immediately suspended in the air, causing her queue and scalp to be completely ripped off. The blood and flesh were dripping, a tragic sight that was unbearable to witness. She died before she could be rescued..." Such tragic machine killings can often be seen in newspapers. But people in society seem to pay no attention. It feels like the saying "human life is like an ant" is not an excessive statement. I was moved and saddened, so I wrote this warning text. I would also like to propose a method, hoping that the municipal authorities will seriously crack down. Notify all large and small factories in this city that all female workers with queues must have their queues cut off. The factory should also set a rule that female workers must cut off their queues, otherwise they will be suspended from work. In this way, for the sake of their livelihoods, they will naturally cut off their queues. Then, danger can be avoided and the lives of many poor and weak women can be saved. It would be an immeasurable virtue. I hope that the factory managers will urge and implement it!

Miscellaneous Talk

Research on Inkstones (27) 277

— Wuliao Ke (Bored Guest)

Other Famous Inkstones

2. Tao River Green

Among green stones, Tao River stone is the most valuable. Previous people who used green stone for inkstones used about five kinds: 1. Tao River stone, 2. Duanxi stone, 3. Songhua stone, 4. Pujiang stone, 5. Yu Xi stone. Pujiang stone comes from Sichuan, and Yu Xi stone comes from Chenzhou. Both are smooth but do not grind ink well, and the color is not very pleasing. So, I won't discuss them in detail. The green stone of Songhua River was called the best in Xie's "Research on Inkstones." After Kangxi obtained this tribute stone, he immediately ordered craftsmen to make a large number of green inkstones, all based on the stone style, with detailed carvings. It was popular in the palace for a while. Kangxi also said that its material was firm and warm, the color was beautiful and bright, the texture was brilliant, and it felt like it was about to drip when held. Therefore, he cherished it very much. However, it was only the emperor's temporary likes and dislikes. The stone was ultimately not as fine and moist as Duanxi. Those that circulated outside were also not seen to be very practical. As for the green stone of Duanxi, the Water Rock is also the best, called the saint of Duan inkstones, there is no objection. However, Tao River green before the Song Dynasty was surprisingly good at grinding ink, and because it was in a large river, it was extremely difficult to obtain, so it was regarded as the most important of the green stones at the time.

The texture of Tao stone Tao River is a tributary of the Yellow River in Lintao Prefecture, Shaanxi. Tao green stone is produced in the deep waters of this large river. It is impossible to investigate when it was discovered and mined. Most of the Tao stones seen by later generations are objects from before the Song Dynasty. Because the riverbed had already changed by the Song Dynasty, the stone veins at the previous mining sites could no longer be traced. Therefore, there are very few Tao River inkstones passed down in the world. The most valuable stone color is the one that has a blue color on a blue-green background, followed by green mixed with yellow or yellow spots. What is especially different from other green stones is that Tao green stone must have the tendons of Duan stone's banana leaf white, similar to the appearance of a freshly unfolded banana leaf with dew, with no slight difference. All those with tendons must have a sharp edge, so it grinds ink differently from other inkstones. Huang Shangu wrote a poem for Zhang Wenqian: "I give you Tao green containing wind ripples, it can temper the brush tip as sharp as a cone." Zhang and Shangu's poem said: "A bright window tests ink, showing moisture, Duanxi and Shezhou have no such color." Chao Wugui wrote a poem with Shangu: "A Taozhou stone is more valuable than two Zhao Bi jades, the duck head of the Han River has no such color." Yang Xinxiang's poem said: "I only see the moth green carved in Linzhou, why use the Mei Zi of Shexi?" All of this is enough to prove that the ancients cherished Tao stone.

Finance One Day in the Gold Market, There Was Little Difference in Fluctuation International Telegrams Were More Favorable to Sellers After Twisting and Turning, There Was a Slight Drop of One Cent 278

Yesterday, the market at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange continued to be sluggish. Throughout the day, the market was supported in the morning opening by the 53rd issue's troop reduction tie-in, with retail investors still showing some appetite, generally bidding slightly better by 5-10 cents. The 20th issue, having fallen significantly the previous day, rebounded by 40 cents. In the second session, the 4th issue alone sold the 20th issue, causing it to quickly retrace by a small 40 cents. Other issues also followed, declining by small margins of 20-30 cents.

In the afternoon sessions, there was still no sign of recovery. Troop reduction bonds fell more significantly due to diminished buying interest, while other bonds also weakened by 10-20 cents per session. At the close, only the near-term troop reduction bonds and the long-term salt tax bonds improved slightly by 5-10 cents. There was no sign of a return to bullishness.

The settlement date has been set for the 27th. With only four trading days remaining in the current month, major short sellers are unlikely to roll over their positions, which is a matter of great concern for future market infighting. Uneven Performance in New York Stock Market 283

The Canadian government's plan to impose a 10% tax on domestically produced gold led to a sharp decline in gold and silver mining stocks. Simultaneously, a renewed sharp drop in wheat prices put pressure on the stock market. Later, President Roosevelt agreed to meet with Senate silver advocates to discuss silver issues, causing silver stocks to rebound quickly.

Wheat once plunged by 5 cents due to Agriculture Secretary Wallace's prediction that US wheat prices would reach parity with world wheat prices within the year. It is claimed that for US grains to compete with other countries in the world market, the price difference between domestic and Liverpool prices must be eliminated. Corn and oats were strong, and wheat's market position improved due to recent heavy selling by bulls. Therefore, the market turned higher at the end.

The small exchange fell due to weakness in gold mining stocks. US government bonds were mixed, with high-grade bonds stable and foreign government bonds showing mixed gains and losses. According to a report from the bank's agent, the (securities) market remained firm and was unaffected by commodities. (Wheat) Agriculture Secretary Wallace's statement that US wheat prices should reach parity with world prices led to selling by bulls, but strong buying persisted due to unfavorable weather in the Northwest region, making a price decline unnecessary at present. (Cotton) Reports suggest that President Roosevelt and the Senate may reach a compromise on the Dies silver proposal. With wheat finally rebounding, the cotton market ultimately turned higher, but the situation remains uncertain. (Rubber) The market was dull and stable, with very little physical supply. (Sugar) Despite selling by bulls, the market remained stable with a sound market position, and positive news could lead to a rise. (Silver) The opening was unremarkable, but the market rose in the afternoon due to rumors that President Roosevelt had agreed to reconsider the silver legislation issue. Food: Bulls and Factories Aggressively Sell, Wheat Flour Prices Hit Record Low of $1.9889 293

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, prices for all months shifted from a quiet state to a sharp downward trend. This situation had been brewing for many days. However, a part of the factories, constrained by ingrained habits, were unwilling to follow the natural trend and gradually reduce their holdings. Nevertheless, both northern and southern merchants felt that sales were not improving, so they remained unmoved, hovering around 2.05 yuan for more than a month. It was difficult to rise, and there was no way to fall. Until recently, overseas wheat markets continued to decline sharply, which had a profound impact on the local market. Small factories began to sell off, and large factories secretly followed suit. In recent days, the market has seemed to be in a state of panic. Yesterday, because Chicago prices fell by about 1 yuan and Canadian prices fell by 20-30 cents, market sentiment was very weak at the opening. Bulls sold in a frenzy, and factories also reduced their holdings, causing the market to decline step by step. The new low record since the establishment of the exchange has also been revealed. For example, the prices for June, July, August, and September all broke the 2 yuan mark, falling to 1.9889 yuan. This record seems to be following the decline in the prices of various commodities and cannot be avoided anymore.

In the afternoon, the market sentiment of the first three sessions was still weak and soft to the extreme. For example, the price for May also fell to 2 yuan, the price for June fell to 1.9725 yuan, the price for July fell to 1.965 yuan, the price for August fell to 1.975 yuan, and the price for September fell to 1.9875 yuan. The miserable trend was unprecedented. Because the factory sales were not price-limited, the decline was even greater. Later, due to short covering, prices rebounded slightly. According to speculation in the industry, now that the 2 yuan mark has been broken, it would not be surprising even if the price fell to 1.5 yuan. As a result, prices for April, May, and June each fell by 2.5 cents, the price for July fell by 2.25 cents, the price for August fell by 2.75 cents, and the price for September fell by 3.25 cents. The total daily trading volume was also large, reaching 689,000 bags.

Semai Wheat Drops Frequently by 7-8 Points 294

Yesterday, after the opening of the Semai wheat futures market in the morning, prices for all months showed a sluggish trend. Although foreign wheat prices, such as those in Chicago, fell by about 1 yuan and Canadian prices fell by 20-30 cents, the buyers and sellers were holding each other back. Although the trend was not good, the decline only reached 20-30 cents. In the afternoon, the situation suddenly changed drastically. The wheat flour market fell sharply, and both industry insiders and outsiders became very uneasy. The opening price was invisibly reduced by 50-60 cents. Later, it still did not improve. Because delivery was approaching for this month, the supply was abundant, and the wheat flour market lacked actual sales to support it, sentiment was also very poor. By the close, the price for this month had plunged by 8 points, the price for June had fallen by 8 points, the price for July had fallen by 8 points, and the price for August had fallen by 7 points. September had just started trading, and the price was as low as 2.79 yuan. The factory demand for spot wheat was quiet, and there were no cloud wheat purchases.

Spring Silkworms Start, Existing Silk is Still Thick 299

The Zhejiang counties plant new mulberry Hangzhou Heng Silkworm Silk Improvement Committee, in view of the fact that the farmers in the subordinate areas have failed to raise silkworms in recent years, all because the young silkworms are fed poorly, and the silkworm disease is found, leading to the abandonment of leaves halfway, so they specially pre-purchase a large number of improved new mulberry seedlings, and distribute them to farms in various counties, and supply them to the young silkworms according to law. As a result, overseas silk sales have plummeted in recent years, silk prices have plummeted, and prices have also been cheapened accordingly. Silkworm farmers have suffered losses, and their interest in raising silkworms and planting mulberries is lackluster. Now that the Grain Rain Festival is approaching, the silkworm business has started, but there are few people who buy seeds and hatch them.

The export of yellow and white factory warp to the United States is increasingly rare, and the sales of Chinese silk in the United States have plummeted. In the past, 3000-4000 packages of yellow and white factory warp were shipped to New York and other ports every month, but now it has become a crossbow end. This month, the statistics of yellow and white factory warp shipped from Shanghai to the United States are only 85 packages.

The sales of foreign silk are extremely sluggish. The price of New York existing silk has repeatedly plummeted, and the price of British Chinese silk is also difficult to stand. The European and American villages in Shanghai do not dare to stomach and risk buying white factory warp. Chinese silk merchants are willing to endure the pain to lower the price to seek sales, because the spring silkworms have started and the existing silk is thick. However, the sales of silk are extremely sluggish, and the future has fallen into a desperate situation.

Free Talk

New York Correspondence (II) 301

— Luo Ailan

If you like to watch movies, you can also see the news that spring is coming in the movies. You don't have to spend a lot of money to go to the grand cinema of Muai Hall, you can also see it in a small theater in Harlem for a dime. After entering the venue, when the newsreel is shown, you can see the exhibition of new spring clothes. There are several beautiful women, wearing new spring clothes with new patterns, with smiles (although you can see from the expression that the mouth smiles but the heart does not smile, this smile is bought with money). They sway down from a very gorgeous staircase. A woman with a French accent tells you from the side that this is the new spring outfit of this year, and it is a new style from Paris. Undoubtedly, spring is coming.

After watching the movie, if you want to buy a box of thumbtacks, or a bundle of stationery, when you go to a 151 company, you will see a corner dedicated to selling flower seedlings. There are various flower seedlings placed there, with the patterns of various flowers in full bloom printed on the paper bags. Next to it are flower pots, flower hoes, and soil (you have to pay for the soil, you may not believe it, but this is New York). There are many fat old women surrounding a female shop assistant dressed in the fairy costume of the "God of Spring", asking about the cultivation methods of various flower seedlings. If you go to a larger department store such as Macys, on the fifth floor, you can also see the Garden Show. They have specially displayed a small scene of a garden for you, and many flower seedlings moved out of the "warm room" are sprouting. A breath of spring's wet mud rushes into your nose, which is tantamount to telling you: "Spring has come to the world."

If you don't watch movies, fortunately or unfortunately you have a wife, and you don't need to run to department stores, at least you have to read the newspaper, and the newspaper will also reveal the news of spring. In the sports column, someone reports that the Giauls or Yaukee baseball team has started practicing somewhere, or a jade photo of the baseball king Raby Rulh holding a bat. That means spring is coming, because spring is the time for them to practice. The news of the departure of the circus is also a symbol of spring coming; but the most accurate one should be the reader's letter column. If you find someone writing from a small village more than a hundred miles away from New York, saying that he heard the first robin's call this morning, then undoubtedly spring has come. You may suspect that the readers of this small village want to show off in big newspapers, and they didn't hear the robin's cry at all, or they didn't wake up from a hangover and took the cat's meow as a bird call, but the editor is willing to publish this letter, which is clear evidence that spring has arrived.

Sometimes, unfortunately, you stayed in Downtown for too long, and didn't take the subway back until around 5 pm. The car is crowded with male and female employees who have just left the office. At that moment when you can't breathe, there is a woman across from you, with her jade hands that have been typing all day, holding high the leather strap in the car, and with a handbag under her armpit. In that face that is over-fatigued, there is a half-smile that suddenly appears. Although this smile disappears soon, you don't know where it came from, and you don't know where it went, but this is clear evidence that spring has arrived. It's like a whirlpool that suddenly floats up in a pond in spring water, both of which are the pranks of the god of spring.

Women are the most intentional disseminators of the god of spring. You see them wearing the newest clothes, walking the most brisk steps, humming the most popular tunes, and sending out the amorous feelings in the corners of their eyes everywhere. That means: Spring is almost ripe. Those who have lovers should go find their lovers quickly, and those who don't have lovers may as well go to Central Park to run alone. There, couples are everywhere, and the spring is full of ponds and ripe on the trees. If you have an acquaintance who works in the city government and happens to be in charge of issuing marriage certificates, you may as well make a phone call to him at this time to try it out. He is sure to answer you: "Too busy, no time to talk."

Who says New York doesn't have spring?!

On "Literary Sketches" and "Humor" 302

— By

I don't know why literary sketches have been criticized as if they were a crime. However, advocates of literature focus solely on sketches, considering them "the only success of Chinese literature in the past fourteen years." Why make such a fuss? Literary sketches are just that – literary sketches.

Undoubtedly, "literary sketches" are sometimes also "great literature" ("Great scholars produce great literature!" - Author's note). The power of a long article sometimes cannot match that of a short sketch. It's worth promoting! (Mr. Lin, upon hearing this, should present me with a silver cigarette case.) Moreover, often it is a few cold, short words that stir up great storms, and often it is latent thoughts that disturb society.

Those who attack sketches probably don't understand: the way things are said varies depending on the environment. In a "salon," it is best not to shout slogans, and when writing love letters, it's best not to copy sociology lecture notes. Articles are written by all sorts of people, presenting all sorts of characters. Even those who are like-minded sometimes cannot tolerate each other. To insist that everyone create literature according to the materialist view of history, or that everyone write like Gorky, would ultimately be quite lonely.

Therefore, it's no big deal that Mr. Lin indulges in literary sketches alongside "humor." He certainly wouldn't force today's literary giants to each write a "sketch" or tell a "humorous" story. For example, if Mr. Lin smokes a cigar (though he probably doesn't smoke them much), and young people upon seeing this, throw off their sleeves and rush to the tobacco company, wouldn't that be too naive?

Of course, saying that we are now in the "age of the literary sketch" is also permissible, as there isn't any grand era to speak of. The current time is indeed suitable for the flourishing of literary sketches. As the winter snow begins to melt, and faint traces of green appear from the scorched earth, a few scattered small flowers and grasses embellish the boundless scenery. Although foreshadowing the future, for now, perhaps that is all there can be.

Subjectively speaking, the great literature of our time is something like "children picking fragrant herbs." However, "Ren Jian Shi" (This Human World) does gather together the greatest literary talents in the country, from "Mr. Cai" to Quan Zenghu. The characters are, at least, all present. However, to produce such a "Ren Jian Shi"! Some things are just not "humorous". Perhaps "it starts simply, but will end grandly," and the future will be different. "'Living in a house out of necessity, that's all there is to it!'"

After Marriage 303

— Yi Ping

The telephone on my desk rang.

"Is that Mei Jun...? Please come to my house at five o'clock; he wants to meet you... Is something up? Can't you come?... You must come, you must come! (Laughing sound)"

Looking at the clock on the wall, it was already four-thirty. I quickly tidied up the documents on my desk. Smoking a cigarette, I pondered the question of whether to go or not. She had been married for almost a month, and during this month, there had been no news from her. It seemed as if she had long forgotten our former secret pact. However, it was good to have discarded something that had been weighing on my mind. But today's phone call seemed to be the result of careful planning, or perhaps she had been suffering from this matter for a long time this past month. Thinking this way, I decided to make the trip, as it wouldn't be a loss for me regardless. After getting off the tram, I found the address she had given me. It was a small Western-style house inside the lane. I went up and rang the doorbell. A young maid opened the door. I told her I was visiting Mr. and Mrs. XXX.

"Please go upstairs; Madam has been waiting for a long time." The young maid answered mechanically.

Before I could consider anything, Yun's laughter came from upstairs. "Mei Jun, come upstairs." A month of married life had completely changed her attitude.

She was wearing a silk nightgown, as if she had just woken from an afternoon nap. She shook hands with me at the top of the stairs and led me to her room.

"Hasn't he returned yet?" I asked, taking the cigarette she offered me. "He'll be back in a little while." She said with a smile, turning toward the back room.

I looked around the room and sat on the sofa by the window.

"It's been a long time." She came out of the back room, having changed into a bright red cheongsam. Before her marriage, I had said that this was the most well-tailored dress. Now, it seemed somewhat tighter. Seeing that my cigarette wasn't lit, she quickly lit a match for me.

"Thank you, it has been a long time."

"Are you still at that company?" she asked, retreating to the desk chair.

"Yes." After I said that, I remembered that she had called my company, or perhaps she was just asking casually. I picked up a collection of XXX photographs on the desk and flipped through them randomly. On the last page, I saw a photograph titled "Old Man," showing an old man hammering iron. I seemed to have seen it somewhere before, but I couldn't remember where. I looked up and pondered for a moment.

"Life has such moments," she said, as if guessing my thoughts. "Yes, have you seen 'Life'?"

"I went to the opening day at Jin Cheng; it was done very well."

"Oh, you told me that. Didn't your sister lose a handbag that day?"

"Then why did you ask me!" she said, laughing and casually taking a cigarette to smoke.

The young maid brought in a cup of tea and retreated, just as mechanically.

"Why hire such a servant?"

"It's a little better!" she said, smiling triumphantly.

The small clock in front of the bed struck six.

"He hasn't come back yet?"

"He'll be back in a little while."

"Is it like this every day?"

Haha, she laughed loudly, inexplicably, "Why should I want him to come back? Someone is treating him to dinner tonight; how could he possibly come back?" She turned her head to look at the closed door and said,

"Such airs, I couldn't get you to come here without begging!" She jumped up from the chair and sat on the desk.

"Come here to do what?"

"What about today?"

I didn't answer; what could I say? I couldn't believe that a woman could become so bold after marriage. I stared at the photograph collection in my hands. It was as if the old man had raised the iron hammer and was striking it down with hatred, and it seemed as if he was striking a certain part of my body.

"Why don't you speak? I'm asking you, what did you come here to do today?" She put both legs on my body, something she had never done in all the years we had known each other.

"I have something to do; I think I should go." I stood up, pretending to be calm.

"Can't you stay for dinner?" she said, also seeming serious. "I'll trouble you next time."

"How polite!"

I reached out and shook her hand, hurrying downstairs, almost taking the photograph collection with me.

"Mei Jun, I won't see you off."

I saw her blow a kiss at the top of the stairs, looking somewhat melancholy.

Mom (2) 305

— Luo Hong

"Do you love Mom?... "

"Brother says Mom can make foreign desserts. Li Gu, have you ever eaten them?" The girl, Wu, pointed to the photograph, her cheeks flushed and smiling.

Her charming appearance made her father feel she was particularly adorable, so he picked her up and gently kissed her on the forehead.

"Dad, you said just now, where are we going?" she said, patting her father's neck.

"Ah, you never forget these things!" The father held her a little tighter. The four of them went to the park together. On the way home, they each held one of their father's hands, truly enjoying the rare moment of happiness, and the father was also very happy.

"Dad, who is Li Gu?" the older child asked.

The father looked at both children and then slowly said,

"Do you like her?"

"I like her, Dad," the girl said.

"I'll tell you, she's going to be your mom..." The father hesitated for a moment, finally saying this in a somewhat unnatural voice.

"Mom?" the older child asked in surprise, looking at his father's face.

At this moment, the father was also looking at the child's face. The child's surprise made him feel a little uneasy.

"Yes, don't you often feel unhappy because you don't have a mom? If Li Gu becomes your mom, she will surely love you."

The children were silent. The girl only felt that this was a truly new and exciting thing. She still remembered Li Gu's smile when she gave her a box of chocolates, and she also remembered Li Gu caressing her head and small hands with affection. The older child, although he also saw Li Gu's warmth, felt somewhat unnatural at the thought of a stranger coming to be his mom. And when he heard that Li Gu would be his mom, he couldn't help but think of his own mom. He still remembered his mom's appearance and caresses very clearly. Thinking of all this, he looked at his father beside him and lowered his head without saying a word.

West Tianmu Daily Log (8) 306

— Yu Dafu

Another rock nose, where there is a Four-Faced Buddha pavilion built on a sheer cliff, is a little east of the Upside-Down Lotus position, and faces the Upside-Down Lotus from across a deep valley. The scenery seen from the Four-Faced Buddha Pavilion looking east and south is similar to that seen from the Upside-Down Lotus. However, on this rock nose, you can look west and down at the entire mountain and temples within the West Tianmu Mountain region, which is also a worthwhile view.

From the Four-Faced Buddha's rock nose, go back and slightly east up to Half Moon Pond. One mile further east is Dragon Pool (or Dragon Pond), and the Eastern Gate's Stone of the Waiting Wife. Because we were hungry and our legs were a little tired, we only went as far as Half Moon Pond.

After eating lunch in the Kaisan Hall, we slowly walked down the mountain. After walking three or five miles, we turned east from the mountainside and surprisingly arrived above a flat area below the Four-Faced Buddha cliff. This place is called Dongwuping. The pagoda of Yulin (also written as Lin) National Master, the founder of the Chanyuan Temple, is located here. The tomb inscription reads: "Pagoda of the Thirty-First Generation Yulin Xiu Master."

From Dongwuping, continue west and south to descend the mountain. After reaching the Five Mile Pavilion, we returned along the original path. By the time we returned to Chanyuan Temple, our lodging from the previous night, it was already a little after four in the afternoon. We met Yutang again, and everyone exaggerated hundreds of times how good the scenery was up there, how good it was. Needless to say, we added many more Dichtungs to the Wahrheit, the purpose of which was nothing more than to make Yutang feel a little regretful. This is another proof of the evil of human nature. But Yutang is also a great Dichter, and he was unwilling to show weakness, so he also had his own Diechthung.

In the evening, we naturally stayed in the guest room of Chanyuan Temple.

After spending two nights and one day at Chanyuan Temple in West Tianmu, we had roughly seen the face of West Tianmu. However, we were far from being able to explore its depths and mysteries. However, we had already tasted the six wonders of Tianmu that Yuan Zhonglang spoke of: flying springs, strange rocks, hermitage temples, cloud peaks, large trees, and tea shoots. The only regret was that there was no thunder and rain, so we did not hear the infant-like thunder. Guangdan and Zenghu were also eager to win, saying, "Yuan Zhonglang never saw ice pillars!" This was indeed true.

Chanyuan Temple in West Tianmu has a great deal of farmland, and therefore a considerable annual income. The donations of the believers and the income from the water and land ceremonies amount to more than ten million yuan a year, even if we count conservatively. There is, of course, no problem for the thatched huts all over the mountain and the two or three hundred monks in the temple to eat and wear clothes. As for the internal organization of the temple and the monks' sexual desires, etc., these are probably Guangdan's favorite topics. In this place, I can only omit them.

(Traveling to East Tianmu)

March 31, Saturday, clear but not bright.

We got up at eight in the morning. After breakfast, we took sedan chairs from Chanyuan Temple and went east. We crossed Panlong Bridge, traversed Zhu Tou Tuo Ridge, passed Sunrise Peak, and descended to a valley. We walked along a stream, which is a tributary of the Dongguan Creek originating from the North Pit of Ni Ridge. The valley in the fan that we looked down on yesterday from the Upside-Down Lotus is the area of Jiadeqian Township. When we arrived at this place, our group had become figures in a fan painting. The two Tianmu Mountains are about thirty miles apart. Starting from the west and heading east, we passed the steep rocky mountains of Liujiao Ridge (commonly known as) and Men Ridge, and then arrived at the new stream in Xizhen of East Tianmu. There is a Zhaoming Hermitage at the foot of the eastern mountain. We got out of the sedan chair to rest for a while and looked at an ancient Wenxuan plaque and a small Prince Pagoda. We then went up the mountain again. After walking ten miles, we could see the bell tower and Scripture Dividing Terrace of the East Tianmu Zhaoming Temple.

This time, we came down at Zaoxi Station and went to West Tianmu first, then went backwards to East Tianmu. If you want to go to East Tianmu first, you should get off at Hualong Station and go north for thirty miles to reach it. In short, whether you go east first and then west, or west first and then east, if you want to visit these two famous mountains and enjoy a tour of western Zhejiang, you must pass through the large valley between the two mountains, and the three ridges, several streams, and four or five villages. Peach blossoms and plum blossoms, pines and firs, interspersed with bamboo and trees; square fields, surrounded by flowing water; high mountains on three sides, sloping down to the south, the southern mountains looming, like subjects and servants paying homage to the northern star. Speaking of this wonderful rural scenery between the East and West Tianmu Mountains, it is indeed somewhat lovely.

The Tianmu mountain foot east of the Zhaoming Hermitage is commonly called Tiger's Tail. We reached a small mountain ridge at the Five Mile Pavilion. From here, we went up the mountain in a winding path, one pavilion every mile. After passing Pinhu Stone and Suiyu Slope, we could see the East Cliff Waterfall below the East and West White Dragon Pools on the side of the Snail Winding Road. The waterfall hangs between two peaks and is still several dozen feet high when viewed from a distance. The sound of the waterfall is faintly like thunder, but it can only be seen and not reached. Because we were limited by the date, we could not slowly search for secluded and adventurous places. Therefore, we only paid a distant respect to this East Cliff Waterfall on the road.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Musings

Yarn Factory Relief Plan 308

— Mei Zhongyi

The reason for the sluggishness of Chinese yarn may not be entirely as stated in the letter, or perhaps what is stated is just one aspect of the issue. The author, being an employee of a yarn factory, seems to speak more intimately, and moreover, Chinese-owned factories, not just yarn factories, probably inevitably follow this kind of situation. This is a common habit of Chinese industrialists. Therefore, I have hastily recorded Mr. Mei's letter below for reference. - Reporter's Note

Recently, newspapers have frequently reported that Chinese yarn factories are unable to sustain themselves and will be handed over to banks for management or will implement wage cuts and shutdowns. However, when we examine the root causes, the reason why Chinese yarn factories are not thriving is due to the dumping and encroachment of Japanese yarn. However, in most cases, the factory itself is unaware of the need for improvement!

The author is also an employee of a yarn factory and knows a thing or two about the yarn industry. Now, seeing that our national yarn factories are declining rapidly, I cannot bear to sit idly by and watch them collapse. Therefore, I dare to present the corrupt situation of the factories below, hoping that the manufacturers will quickly rise up, eliminate accumulated shortcomings, and then the future development will be limitless. A gain or a loss, I pray that our manufacturers deeply consider this!

A. Employees' positions are not based on merit.

B. Managers and senior employees are corrupt in their work:

(1) Too arrogant, domineering

(2) Not punctual; office hours start at nine, but they leisurely arrive at ten; some don't even get up at noon, and their presence is not seen until two or three in the afternoon

(3) Do not provide any guidance or training to lower-level employees.

C. The factory's rewards and punishments for workers are unclear.

D. Do not strictly inspect the raw cotton (resulting in inferior quality goods).

E. The machines are old, resulting in slow production and increased wages. Employees are not hired based on merit, and many are introduced through personal connections, with connections to powerful and influential figures. They work carelessly and do not personally visit the factory floor to investigate and research, resulting in numerous waste. They misuse flying flowers, and the quality of the goods often does not match the appearance. As for the shipping of goods to customer brokers, factory fees are added, amounting to about three to five jiao per package, which is detrimental to the buyer's cost. The most hateful thing is that if the sales of customer brokers are slightly active, they will raise the market price and hold on tight, allowing Japanese yarn to be dumped into the market because customer brokers need the supply and have no other option. The factory's runners also elevate their status and are unable to be humble with brokers and customer brokers, and they often engage in private corruption, setting up their own companies to manipulate the factory's market prices. The reason why customer sales are slow is due to these people. As a result, inventory accumulates day by day, and the factory has no way to sell it. They negotiate with banks or money houses to mortgage it, and the factory constantly pays interest. Day after day, month after month, the factory's burden increases invisibly, leading to the saying that they are unable to sustain themselves. However, empty talk of relief is of no help. If the factory does not fundamentally improve, eliminate accumulated shortcomings, and eliminate bad habits, how can it lift the heavy burden from its shoulders? Regarding foreign merchants: they start work at eight o'clock and often visit the factory floor to investigate and research. They have clear rewards and punishments for workers. When they encounter customer sales, they try their best to accommodate them and often adhere to the principle of small profits and quick turnover. They are often available for negotiations even after five o'clock. They do not work as carelessly as we do in our country. According to what my friends have told me, "Foreign merchants mostly made profits last year." Looking back at our country's yarn factories, how are they doing?

The author is not praising others' prestige and diminishing our own ambition. High-sounding talk of relief and empty shouting are the actions of a fool. The fundamental thing is to encourage ourselves, otherwise, we should be wary of having our position seized in the future. A gain or a loss, please deeply examine this.

Man and Society 309

— Construction

We should have collective activities

Sometimes, a kind person often wants to turn their own feelings into other people's feelings, and replace other people's thoughts with their own thoughts. This is difficult and unreasonable, but sometimes it is truly moving because of the promotion of that kind of sincerity. This kind of person is lovely, but only lovely.

The psychology of people who say that something is bad always has a belief in something good. Although they themselves believe this thing is excellent, they cannot resist others denying it and feel that many activities in life are wasted.

However, in my opinion, there is always a truth to everything. Each holding one end does not necessarily mean that both are truths. If not, then we have no right or wrong. Wouldn't that become a chaotic mess?

Regarding participating in social activities, it is originally a matter of differing opinions. Here, I always want to put aside the question of "should or shouldn't" and only ask: are we one of the people?

I think everyone will affirm this point, because no one can say that they are "non-human." If this point is acknowledged, then I want to ask: how does the rice you eat every day come from? Did you cook it? Did you buy it? Did you use a mill to get it from the rice paddy? Did you transport the grain? Did you plant the rice? After asking this, I want to ask, how does the clothes you wear every day come from?... And what about your housing, your entertainment, your reading...?

If a person can think in this way, then they will realize that life and society cannot be separated. Without society, one cannot unfold their life.

However, society cannot be formed by one person. It requires a large group of people, many people, to organize it. A society that has been organized has a function, and all individuals in the society must adhere to the principle of division of labor and cooperation, each doing their best. However, individual forces that are separated have little effect. They must be subject to the function of the society, and the scattered individuals must become a collective force. Only by engaging in social production with this collective force can there be any talk of the happiness of all of humanity. Then we as individuals can also have our own safety and individual happiness.

Therefore, a person who wants their own safety and their own happiness must recognize that they are a member of the people, that their safety and happiness are tied to the safety of society and the happiness of humanity. If we recognize this point, then is it necessary for us to participate in group activities for the safety and happiness of our entire society?

Should or shouldn't, it seems to be psychological. I won't talk about it for the moment. I just want to make this point: society includes all of us. We cannot live as isolated individuals. For the sake of our own lives, our own safety, and our own happiness, why don't we participate in these general group activities that guarantee our lives and promote our society?

Therefore, regarding debates about morality, about so-called "despicable behavior," "treacherous hearts," "backstabbing," "practice of political skills," "preparation for betrayal," etc., I feel that there is no need to debate. As long as the major premise is clear, what does it matter if there are some unsatisfactory flaws in the current situation? Isn't it just a matter of changing them? But if someone fundamentally opposes participating in group life because of this, I am somewhat suspicious that they have been poisoned by some kind of venom.

Sex Education 310

— Jing Jia

It is a mistake to look at anything with a mysterious eye. If there is a fact in the world, there can never be any possibility of secrecy.

People generally think that matters between the sexes are extremely mysterious. Whenever their children ask about matters between the sexes, they will stop them. In fact, this is a great mistake. The evolution of social civilization is based on the relationship between the sexes. If there were no sexes, there would be no society. Since sex has such a close relationship with ourselves, what secret is there to speak of?

Although there is physiology and hygiene in schools, the extremely important aspect of sex is omitted. In the course of life, sex is a very serious problem. Everyone has to go through a sexual life, but because no one guides them, they often rush about like blind people riding horses, thus creating dangerous and tragic endings.

I am a student, so of course I understand things about students better than others, so I will take the student aspect as an example. Middle school is the time when an individual's sexual needs are most urgent. At the time of complete development, sexual desire is at its strongest. On the one hand, young people want to satisfy their desires, and on the other hand, no one is there to guide them on a proper path, so abnormal solutions to sexual desires are produced, such as masturbation and homosexuality. It is almost impossible to find a student who does not play these tricks. As a result, sexual diseases such as spermatorrhea, impotence, and nocturnal emission are produced! Judging from the "beautiful" advertisements for sexual diseases in newspapers and on toilet walls, I don't know how many sexual disease patients there are in China!

We know that the strength of the people affects the strength of the country. Since there are so many sexual disease patients in China, the women produced will not be strong. If this continues, the Chinese nation will inevitably be eliminated by the survival of the fittest and perish.

This is entirely the result of ignoring sex education!

Newspapers and magazines have repeatedly called for sex education, but no one has paid attention to it so far. Perhaps "sex" is detrimental to social customs!? Perhaps the officials in charge believe that sex education is unimportant? Chinese people are always the Chinese people of the "land of propriety and righteousness"!

I hope that the education authorities will pay attention to this issue. I hope that what is studied in schools is not only a review of academic theories. I dare to earnestly ask that "sex education" be listed as one of the required courses, even if someone calls me Zhang Jingsheng the Second, it doesn't matter.

Cold-Blooded World 311

— Construction

"The world is cold-blooded!" I shout this, and affirm it so.

Lower beings say so much; now, the world is strangely cold-blooded, with no sincerity in sight, no intimacy, all hideous faces, all vicious hearts.

Ordinary fields need not be mentioned; friends framing friends, confidants framing confidants, in joyous meetings, it seems that sharp knives are flying, it seems that pistols are aiming. Yet on the surface, they are so smiley-faced, how cruel and cold-blooded this is! Between father and son, husband and wife, brothers and sisters, originally united by blood, originally related as if their lives depended on each other, how intimate and sincere they should be. But in this cold-blooded world, where is intimacy and sincerity? Are they not all like strangers on the road? Are they not all like combatants on the battlefield? Just look at the daily newspapers, your eyes are filled with this kind of cold-blooded performance, what with murdering one's own husband, what with forcing one's daughter into prostitution, what with nephews slaying aunts, etc... As for brothers treating each other as enemies, it is simply the norm.

This world, this world, has truly reached its end; who says that humans are emotional animals? Where are the emotions?

The connection between people depends entirely on self-interest. If their interests are the same, they mingle together; otherwise, they will meet each other with knives and guns.

Because of this, I fear to see the state of lower beings, because although they are lower beings, they want to love each other so much, but we humans, the more advanced we become, the more barbaric, the more cold-blooded.

However, are we to curse the evolution of mankind? That is not an enlightened position.

We must restore the pure connection between people. We desperately need salvation!
